British Secretary of War Gives a Speech, Saying Britain's Military Strength is Insufficient

Feeling a Lack of Both Soldiers and Military Equipment 21

(London) Secretary of War Halesham gave a speech here last night, strongly arguing that Britain's military preparations are insufficient. Halesham said, "Our country feels a lack of both soldiers and military equipment. In terms of the source of military equipment supply, our country has previously discussed in detail and determined a policy. The basis of this policy is that we do not need to set up large-scale public arsenals to meet our needs in wartime. We can rely solely on some private munitions factories to provide us with supplies when the need for military equipment unfortunately increases. For this reason, in terms of the situation of military equipment supply, we are today far more backward than we were 20 years ago. However, if we say that the young people of our country today lack courage and patriotism compared to the young people of 20 years ago, then I dare to say that this is not the case. Last Saturday, I was walking in Regent Street when I saw young men and women wearing black shirts marching in formation. There were not many of them, but a large number of police were guarding them. Behind them was an ambulance and many national flags. From this, it seems that people today regard it as an honor to wear uniforms and march in military formation. Although, I certainly know that few uniforms in the world can compare with the uniforms of our British army, and in our country, apart from the King of England's army, there is definitely no other army. What is even more advanced is that most people today tend to be 'aviation enthusiasts', and some even think that air strikes are far more dangerous than land warfare, so we can do without land defenses. Their foolishness is so laughable that it has reached this point. No one in the navy, army, or air force would agree with this fallacy. Although this year's British-Australian air race is enough to make us understand the actual capabilities of air strikes, it cannot be said that protecting our country does not require relying on the army. On the contrary, the army's use for defense will become even more important. Once we unfortunately have to go to war, in order to deal with air strikes, both land forces and air forces are equally necessary." (25th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

Médéa, France Former Prussian military officer, blind man Larsick, Mr. Vollischmann, and Mr. Krebbs were recently arrested for espionage. According to the prosecutor, in March of this year, the police arrested a Frenchman named Albar, whose behavior was suspicious. He confessed that he had been forced by poverty to supply information to a certain foreign country, which was secretly transmitted orally outside of France. Therefore, the police ordered Albar to telegraph Larsick to meet at a cafe within the French border, saying that there was special good news to tell. Larsick and his companion arrived as scheduled in a large car. As they were talking, the police suddenly appeared from their hiding places and arrested them. After the trial today, Larsick was sentenced to 18 months in prison, and Krebbs, the mastermind of the entire case, was sentenced to five years in prison. Both plan to appeal. Roosevelt Announces Right-Leaning Economic Policy

Calls for Unity in All Industries to Achieve Recovery; No Direct Expression on Currency Issues 29

(Washington) President Roosevelt, in a speech to the American Bankers Association today, called on all sectors of agriculture, industry, and commerce to unite and maintain the traditional economic system of the United States. The President also expressed his approval of profit-making in all industries and denied the "New Deal" socialization theory. Regarding monetary policy, while he stated that there was no intention to engage in further aggressive expansion, he made no specific guarantees. On the crucial issues of stabilizing finance, establishing a government-controlled central bank, and balancing the budget, the President offered no words to comfort public expectations. However, those who heard the speech generally believe that the President has shifted to the right, and the future is somewhat reassuring. The President's tone was very moderate, and he urged bankers to take responsibility for the people and restore their faith. Observers interpreted this as a challenge to financial giants. Regarding the monetary issue that banks had hoped the President would clarify, the President vaguely stated that countries are increasingly eager for price stability, which is also the national policy of various countries. Regarding the need for large sums of money to relieve unemployment, the President said, "After commercial recovery and prosperity, this burden will be lightened." He expressed optimism about the progress of the recovery and said that the government is making every effort to promote public investment. The President explained his concept of government, saying that the old notion of a banker and the government each acting independently and not conspiring with each other has become a thing of the past. The government is the external representation of the common life of all citizens, so the government should lead and judge the interests of various conflicts in society, and bankers are no exception. After vehemently denying the red scare of the New Deal, the President declared, "True national wealth is not a static thing. When everyone cooperates, the national wealth increases day by day. When there is misunderstanding and suspicion, the national wealth stagnates. The United States has the material resources to increase true wealth. Americans believe that true wealth is the reward for mental and physical labor, which is the so-called profit-making system." The President expressed satisfaction with American businessmen's attention to national affairs. The President also pointed to last year's banking crisis as the process by which American banks have achieved their current stable position, and believes that today is a mature opportunity for all industries to unite and achieve commercial recovery, and said that the people are generally expecting us to do our job well. (National Telegram, 24th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt delivered a speech at the annual meeting of the American Bankers Association last night, and Treasury Secretary Morgenthau also delivered a speech this morning. In his speech, the President still advocated the private capital system and did not admit that there was a tendency towards socialism in the "New Deal". Some people were disappointed that the President would not explain the policy in detail, but most financial leaders were very satisfied that the President had indicated that he did not intend to engage in further aggressive expansionary policies. Although the President's speech did not directly discuss the issue of stabilizing the currency, his tone was moderate and he allowed the banking community to say that once private capital shows its willingness to respond to the industry's confidence in lending, the government's lending activities can be stopped. The government still needs to continue lending, but it is urging the banking community to take this responsibility as soon as possible. (National Society Telegram, 25th)

Gains Strong Support from the Military 30

(Tokyo) The government has decided to appoint Hideo Kodama, an influential member of the House of Peers Research Association, as Minister of Colonial Affairs, and the official announcement was made on the 25th. At the same time, Prime Minister Okada's concurrent position as Minister of Colonial Affairs was removed. (Japan United Press, 25th)

(Tokyo) The decision to appoint Earl Hideo Kodama as the full-time Minister of Colonial Affairs was made with the strong support of the military. The military considered various circumstances and advocated the necessity of setting up a full-time Minister of Colonial Affairs, and the criteria for evaluating candidates should meet the following conditions: (1) a person who is well-versed in local affairs; (2) recognizes the importance of the military in implementing the national policy of Manchuria and cooperates with it; (3) has considerable insight into the situation after resolving the disputes of the Kwantung resident staff. According to this view, the entire department believed that Earl Kodama was the most suitable candidate. As a result of Army Minister Hayashi's advice to Prime Minister Okada, the decision was made. (Dentsu News Agency, 25th)

(Tokyo) Today, the newly appointed Minister of Colonial Affairs, Earl Hideo Kodama, gave the following speech to reporters after the appointment ceremony: It is said that the disputes caused by the opportunity of the Manchurian institution reform by local residents are caused by worrying about the nation's beliefs. Therefore, it cannot be regarded as a general dispute. However, since the issue has been decided by the Cabinet, it will be resolved soon. The government will seek active measures to stop onlookers. Because I am a member of the Cabinet, I have not been able to state my firm aspirations. However, I will definitely strive to unify the unintegrated foreign areas and seek countermeasures in cooperation. (Dentsu News Agency, 25th)

(Tokyo) The new Minister of Colonial Affairs, Hideo Kodama, is the son of Army General Gentaro Kodama. After graduating from Tokyo Imperial University, he served as Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, Director-General of the General Affairs Bureau of the Governor-General of Korea, Chief Secretary of the Terauchi Cabinet, President of the Rewarding Bureau, and Governor of Kwantung. In 1929, he was appointed Director-General of Political Affairs of the Governor-General of Korea, and resigned in 1931. After that, he devoted himself to educational undertakings and is now an influential member of the Research Association. It is said that Kodama has a good relationship with the military, so the colonial administration will surely yield good results in the future. (Japan United Press, 25th)

(Fuzhou) The Eastern Route Army for the attack on Tingzhou is ready and will launch an attack within days. Chiang Ting-wen telegraphed Chen Jitang, requesting that all units of the Southern Route Army cooperate. Because the bandits' weapons are incomplete and ammunition is lacking, they have no countermeasures. According to reconnaissance reports, the puppet Central Military Commission intends to (1) concentrate between Ruijin and Shicheng or near Ruijin and Changting to preserve the puppet Central Soviet Area; (2) if defeated, part of them will be divided into small groups and scattered along the Fujian-Jiangxi border, and part of them will flee to the border between Hunan and Sichuan via Anyuan and Xinfeng. Run on Small Denomination Notes at Tianjin Dazhong Bank 64

(Tianjin) A run on small denomination notes suddenly occurred at Tianjin Dazhong Bank at 10:30 this morning. At the same time, all twenty branch exchange offices of the bank in the city also experienced the same run. The bank immediately obtained tens of thousands of small denomination notes from other banks for exchange. It did not rest at noon, and by the afternoon, the head office had exchanged 90,000 notes, and the various exchange offices had exchanged 20,000 notes. In order to maintain its credit, the bank decided to continue exchanging notes overnight until 11:00 PM. According to Sun Jun, the Chief Accountant of the bank, the sudden occurrence of this event is unknown. It is speculated that it may be due to a small number of silver and money merchants deliberately creating this disturbance for profit. (Special dispatch on the 25th)

Summary of Chairman Chiang's Visit to Bian

Yang Yongtai and Soong Mei-ling Travel Together, All Circles in Bian warmly Welcome 86

Kaifeng Correspondence: Since the 10th of this month, news has repeatedly spread in Bian that Chairman Chiang would come to inspect. All agencies and schools were rushing to prepare a welcome, and were very busy. On the 14th, all the main roads once hung cloth banners to welcome Chiang Kai-shek. However, heaven was not kind, and heavy rain fell, discoloring the new cloth and blurring the handwriting. On the 18th, representatives from various agencies were again recommended to establish a welcoming preparatory committee. This morning (today, the 23rd), "Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who defends against bandits and resists insults," "Chairman Chiang Kai-shek who protects the nation," "Welcome Chairman Chiang Kai-shek who is hardworking and meritorious," "Welcome Chairman Chiang Kai-shek who promotes traditional morality" and other slogans have been properly posted and hung on all main roads. Liu Zhi, Chairman of the Provincial Government, Hong Ludong, Special Commissioner of Party Affairs, and Du Jun, Acting President of Henan University, went to Zhengzhou at 5:00 AM to greet him. At about 9:00 AM, the Public Security Bureau ordered all businesses and households to hang the national flag. Soon, representatives from various government agencies and schools formed teams and went to the train station to wait eagerly. At about 12:00 PM, all civil servants and students stood upright outside the station. Subsequently, various Party, government, and military dignitaries arrived one after another. The number of cars parked was unprecedented in Bian. Traffic order was maintained by the Suijing Battalion, armed police from the Public Security Bureau, and the 60th Division. Security was tight. On the platform, in addition to the leaders of various agencies, reporters from various newspapers, and a military band, there were no idlers. At 12:50 PM, two planes flew in from the west, circling in the sky. More than 5,000 welcomers immediately craned their necks and looked forward. As the wind picked up and sand swirled, the special train entered the station amid the melodious sound of military music. There were a total of twelve cars. Chiang emerged from the yellow car in the sixth car, wearing a black padded robe and a mandarin jacket. Liu Zhi and Chen Pei, the commander of the 60th Division, accompanied him. After inspecting the troops at the station, Chiang exchanged greetings with the welcomers, re-boarded the car to rest. The troops of the 60th Division left the station first, followed by Yang Yongtai, Chiang Bo-cheng, etc., who rode into the city. Liu Zhi ordered the welcomers outside the station to return to the city, and then re-entered the station and stood by the car. Madam Yang, Madam Liu Zhi, accompanied Soong Mei-ling, etc., got off the car and entered the city. The leaders of various agencies at the station also entered the city upon Liu Zhi's order. Only Liu and a few others remained at the station to wait for Chiang. It was not until 3:00 PM that they got out of the car and entered the city to go to the Provincial Government. (23rd)

Zhang Xueliang Talks About His Impressions of Inspecting the Northwest 87

Hankou Correspondence: Zhang Xueliang followed Chairman Chiang from Hankou to Luoyang on the 9th, then went to Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, and other places for inspection. On the 22nd, he returned to Luoyang with Chairman Chiang. Chairman Chiang went to Zhengzhou, and arrived in Kaifeng on the 23rd. Whether he will go to Beiping or return to Hankou within days has not yet been decided. Zhang, on the other hand, flew south by Ford aircraft from Luoyang on the 12th. On the 23rd, Zhang published his experiences and impressions of his trip to the west, as well as his views on the future development of the Northwest, as follows: "I accompanied Chairman Chiang from Hankou to Luoyang this time to participate in the opening ceremony of the Tenth Military Academy Branch. Then, I took a car from Luoyang to Weinan and then went to Xi'an. I stayed in Xi'an for two days. Due to the rain, I was unable to inspect the entire area. Later, on a good day, I inspected the troops directly under Yang Hucheng, who was about to take office. Chairman Chiang and I both gave separate speeches. Afterwards, I took a plane to Lanzhou and then flew to Ningxia. I stayed there briefly. After returning to Xi'an, and returned to Luoyang, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek immediately set off to Bian. Because I needed to deal with department affairs urgently, I returned to Hankou by plane. In total, I traveled to four provinces on this tour, lasting half a month. My impressions of the inspection are that the greatness of the Northwest is completely different from what I imagined before I went there. I saw the highway built by Zuo Zongtang when he conquered Xinjiang, stretching from Tongguan to the entire Xinjiang region. I heard that at that time, the trees on both sides were lush, the green shade covered the sun, and pedestrians found it extremely convenient. The Great Wall, which stretches across the territory in an endless winding line, and the An Canal and Tang Canal, are all extremely great construction projects. However, the trees on the side of the road have been felled a lot over the years. In recent years, efforts have been made to cultivate and protect them. The buildings in Lanzhou are also very majestic, and their atmosphere is similar to that of Beiping. In the late Qing Dynasty, there was already a woolen mill run by Zuo Zongtang and others, and the Yellow River Iron Bridge, both of which were extremely large in scale. Ningxia, relying on the Helan Mountains to the north and the Yellow River to the east, is especially majestic in shape and is indeed an important military location. Unfortunately, the people are poor and the economy is not as good as in Shaanxi and Gansu. I believe that to develop the Northwest, we must first pay attention to the development of transportation. For example, the Longhai Railway has already been extended to Weinan, and it is expected to reach Xi'an by the end of this year, and it will officially open to traffic on New Year's Day next year. The Xi'an-Pingliang-Lanzhou Highway, completed by the National Economic Commission, is also barely passable, but this is still preliminary work. Further efforts are still needed in the future. I sincerely hope that the people of the country will pay close attention to the Northwest, jointly seek the development of the borderlands, and truly rely on it for the future of the nation." (23rd)

A Glimpse of the Miao Yi Rebellion in Mengzi, Yunnan 88

The Niu Bandit calls himself the Heavenly Emperor, and the Garrison Team will Pacify Immediately

Kunming Correspondence: Mengzi County belongs to the interior and exterior border region. There is a Miao Yi named Niu Wancai who calls himself the Nine Heavens Emperor. In Galami, which belongs to Mengzi County, he privately built a false imperial palace, appointed Ranmin Peng, the son of a pig butcher, as the false Chief of the General Staff, privately engraved and printed talismans, and made flying symbols. He went to the Miao Yi areas belonging to Mengba and Gejie and other districts, spreading rumors and bewitching the public. He successively gathered about a thousand Miao people and bandits. In the area, he disturbed the peace. He also privately appointed Miao Yi Yang, Ya Xiaodehong, etc. as false generals, Huang Lisi, Yang Wanming, etc. as false commanders, Huang Xiaobao, Yang Sanmiaozi, etc. as false elders, Gao Liu, Xiao Huangkai, etc. as false captains, and other Xiao Zhukai and Zhu Xiaosi as false battalion commanders. On September 12, they attacked Lengquan. Fortunately, Li Yizhi, the magistrate of Mengzi County, and gentry and merchants from all walks of life had received news earlier. Because of the urgency of the situation, they telegraphed the headquarters successively, and on the one hand, they discussed with Li Song, the commander of the Independent Second Regiment stationed in Mengzi, the opportunity to suppress the bandits. The regiment commander Li dispatched two battalions of troops and the local defense team to assist in the suppression. Before the bandits attacked Lengquan, they were prepared to block them. When the bandits arrived, they were caught off guard and met head-on. The rabble was scattered, and Feng Qu Tuan led the local militia to guide them to the bandit's nest in Galami on the 17th, burning down the false imperial palace and Shuishui Ke bandit's nest. The details are as follows:

Situation of the Rebellion 89

The bandit leader of this rebellion, Niu Wancai, is from Galami in the Lengquan area. His ancestors had a small legacy, which he squandered, and he was heavily in debt. He fled to other places and did not return for more than a year. Now he suddenly returned, but people did not know where he came from. Niu then took advantage of the remnants of the Miao rebellion in Qiubei, Xiong Peisheng, to incite rebellion in the alien border, and secretly colluded with him to create rumors, saying that the Celestial Master would help him fly swords and the destiny of heaven would return to the Yi and the Han would perish together. He specialized in exhausting the senses in order to advocate rebellion. The ignorant and stubborn Yi and Miao people were easily bewitched. Shuishui Ke Yang Zifan and Mushu Ke Yang Wanming were particularly devout monks, and their disciples were numerous. Niu's wings had already been formed, so he openly spread rumors, saying that the cycle of heaven's fortune was endless and that there was a number of rises and falls, and used the slogan of not paying rent or donating money to call on the Yi and Miao people to join him. Seeing that most of the Yi and Miao people were inclined to him, Niu dyed his skin all over with Miao colors and called himself the Great Emperor, making flags, talismans, and privately printed meanings. He abused official titles, appointing Yang Mufan as a general and Yang Wanming as a great general, Huang Dacong and Du Zi'en as left and right prime ministers. Anyone who could gather more than ten people would be appointed as the name of a captain of a battalion or company. After the rumors spread and the false appointment letters were issued, Xiang Xingshen, also known as Xiang Miao, with the alias Longneck, Li Guotai, Hu Wancai, Xiong Peijin, Lao Dayu, Shi Shibaobao and others, who had been bandits for many years and had escaped being suppressed, relapsed into their old ways and gathered the remaining bandits in response, hoping to take the opportunity to start an incident. The wind and rumors spread, and the people were suspicious and avoided each other. In the early part of September, the bandits set up yellow and white flags in Shuishui Ke Galami and other places, claiming that they would attack Lengquan on September 12 and Mengzi on the 16th. Previously, on September 9, Mu Su Ke Tang Guifang and his brothers Gui Xing and Gui Ji were ambushed and shot to death by the false general Yang Wanming at Xiao'an Yakou on their way back to Lengquan after going to Baojie Street. That night, the regiment attacked his house, killed people, and seized property. The next day, the bandits killed cattle and pigs in Galami and offered sacrifices to the Celestial Master. Many bandits from all over the place, mostly monkey-like Miao Yi, gathered and drew blood together. They advocated sending the false emperor to Beijing to ascend the throne, cutting off large and small roads. On the 11th, An Tingzhi, the captain of the Shuidao detachment of the Baojie regiment, saw that the bandits were too strong to resist, and led his team to Lengquan. When they were marching to Hongpo Jia, the Xiong bandit Peijin disarmed them all.

Process of Suppression 90

The incident had been brewing for many days, and the authorities had not yet received a clear report from the area. On the 11th, the commander of the Independent Regiment stationed in Mengzi, Commander Li, heard the news and urgently ordered Battalion Commander Lu of the Second Battalion to lead a battalion of soldiers to arrive at Lengquan overnight. At 9:00 AM on the morning of the 12th, the bandits gathered more than a thousand people, divided into eight routes, shouting and attacking Lengquan. Battalion Commander Lu led his troops to meet them head-on. By 4:00 PM, the bandits had been defeated and fled to the surrounding mountains. Dozens of bandits were killed. On that day, because the mountain shapes were complex, they did not pursue them thoroughly and temporarily stationed in Lengquan, reporting to Commander Li to send reinforcements to search and suppress them. Upon receiving the report, Commander Li personally led Battalion Commander He of the Second Battalion and two companies of soldiers to Lengquan on the 14th to plan the suppression and appeasement affairs. Zhou, a member of the County Party Department, and Wan Zhu, the deputy director of the Construction Bureau, also went with them to promote appeasement. On the 15th, Commander Li sent two platoons of soldiers to search and suppress in the nearby areas, capturing bandits who had turned against the government. On the 16th, he summoned the township chiefs and gentry of the district for talks, and decided to focus on appeasement work, issuing a notice to appease the displaced people and asking them to return to farming as soon as possible. Those who followed the orders would be treated leniently and would not be investigated. Those who caught bandit leaders who surrendered would be heavily rewarded. On the 17th, he sent the entire Second Battalion to clear and suppress the bandit nests in Shuishui Ke Galami and Sitang, and the bandits chose to hide in the valleys and resist stubbornly. Many bandits were killed, and many guns, cattle, and horses were seized. Niu's brother, Niu San, was captured. One officer and soldier were killed and one was injured. On the 18th, they returned to Lengquan at the same time. The magistrate of Pingbian County also telegraphed asking for troops. On the 19th, Battalion Commander He led two companies of soldiers, the overall moral of the new, to suppress and console them.

Aftermath Work 91

The wisdom of the Yi and Miao people is shallow and ignorant, stubbornly resistant to change. A few unscrupulous elements instigate them from within, causing unrest. If we do not appease them and instead only engage in suppression, it will increase our power without conferring virtue. It is said that eight or nine out of ten of the miscellaneous troops are not rebels, and only a few are the masterminds. If we try to wipe them out completely, then the foolish will only become sacrifices, and the ringleaders may not submit, which will not help the situation in reality.

Chief Li also advocated focusing on appeasement and making suppression secondary. Therefore, at 12:00 noon on the 21st, he convened a mass meeting of the people, attended by more than 400 people. Chief Li first gave a speech, outlining the following points: (1) The Han and Yi people must unite as one. (2) The district chiefs and neighborhood heads must use special methods to arrest criminals such as Niu Wanzhe. (3) Those who return the seized cattle and horses will be allowed to return to their occupations and live in peace. The captured firearms will be sent to the district office for the use of the local defense. (4) Those who followed the rebels will be given a chance to reform, and their past will be pardoned. (5) When the propaganda teams go to distant places, each village must guarantee protection and assist the government's communications.

Then, Committee Members Liang and Zhou discussed the need to eliminate boundaries between the Han and Yi people, promote equality and mutual assistance, the key points of propaganda for the current departure of the propaganda teams, and the importance of focusing on the baojia system to achieve social stability. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 p.m.

That evening, people from various villages came to collect their cattle, horses, wooden combs, and other items. They also came to submit repentance letters and seek pardon. All were soothed and dismissed by Chief Li. On the 21st, Chief Li ordered the 5th Company to stay in Lengquan to protect the farmers' autumn harvest. The remaining troops returned to Meng along with the seal. (October [Day])

Four-Province (Sichuan, Hunan, Guizhou, Guangxi) Military Encirclement and Suppression of He and Xiao's Remnant Bandits

He's Fake Division Commander Guangdong Sheng Was Killed; Xiao's Bandits, Badly Hit, Fled to Minjiachang and Other Places

Yingkou Correspondence: He Long and Su Ke's bandits attempted to enter Sichuan by separate routes to join forces with Xu Xiangqian's remnant bandits. They have been surrounded and suppressed by the troops of Sichuan, Hunan, Guizhou, and Guangxi provinces, and are now trapped. The Sichuan Bandit Suppression Headquarters reported to the Han on the 23rd, detailing the progress of the suppression. The report stated that, according to the telegram from the Da Brigade of the Chen Division, our army had indeed killed He's fake 7th Division Commander Guangdong Sheng in the battle of Shazichang. According to captured bandits, after Sheng's death, the bandits were fierce and difficult to fight. He was seriously wounded, and the fake 21st Regiment Commander Lai Ting was promoted to replace him. The remaining bandits fled to Xiangganxi and Jiaojiawan. Sheng's bandits were routed by the Hunan and Guangxi armies near Shiqian. Some fled to Minjiachang, Jiangkou, and others to Wanren Mountain. The various armies are still encircling and suppressing them. (23rd)

Songjiang 92

The Tobacco Prohibition Committee Reissues Licenses

The issuance of smoking cessation licenses to smokers by the Tobacco Prohibition Committee of this county was completed at the end of September. The number of smokers who received licenses in the county totaled six thousand and sixty-six, which is quite different from the original registered number. This was for the sake of providing relief before the deadline. To prevent these registered but unlicensed smokers from facing legal penalties, it was decided to reissue licenses from the 25th of this month until the end of the month. The registration forms were retrieved and distributed to the district offices, ordering them to issue the licenses nearby. When smokers receive their licenses, they must clearly state their age, appearance, etc., to show solemnity. Those who have not registered but request a license may not be approved.

Jiashan 93

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire, Hostage Escapes Danger

Shao Deyi, a resident of Hongjiatan Yingaobang, was kidnapped on the 9th of this month by a group of bandits. The bandits broke into his house, entered, and took him away. Later, the Shao family received a letter from the bandits demanding 10,000 yuan. Because the county's security force discovered the bandits' location near Wuzhen, the force, led by Team Leader Huang Yao, together with the police force, led by Inspector Chen Zhefu of the Public Security Bureau, traveled by Xinming transport to Wuzhen Zhongtangfang. First, Shao's relative led two people carrying fake money to negotiate the ransom. When the bandits came, a fierce battle broke out. The bandit Zhou Fusheng, 52 years old, was captured alive. At the same time, Shao seized the opportunity to escape. The bandit is now being escorted by the county government to be interrogated.

Suzhou 94

Anti-Japanese General Jiang Minsheng Arrives in Suzhou

Mr. Jiang Minsheng, an anti-Japanese general known for shining shoes, departed from Shanghai this time to promote the anti-Japanese cause in various places. He arrived in Suzhou from Huzhou the day before yesterday and stayed at New Suzhou Hotel No. 75. Yesterday (29th), he was invited by various schools and groups to speak on the issue of Japanese aggression. He will also go to Europe and the United States to promote the cause to overseas Chinese, in order to recover the lost territories of the Northeast provinces as soon as possible.

Wuxi 95

Drug Dealer Executed

The Public Security Bureau of this county, on August 2nd of this year, acting on a secret order from the Department of Civil Affairs, arrested Feng A'ren (61 years old), who was selling drug pills, at Feng Chang's cigarette and paper shop at No. 37 Zhijie Street, West Gate. Sixty-one empty boxes for drug pills, ten bags of Yunshi, and smoking paraphernalia were confiscated. Zhu Gengsheng, an accomplice in selling drug pills, was also arrested in Huocheng Lane. After the bureau's investigation, the case was transferred to the County Tobacco Prohibition Association and then to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters. Ren Lian, the chief of the military law department, interrogated the case and determined that Feng A'ren had committed the crime of violating Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations on the Strict Prohibition of Highly Addictive Drugs and sentenced him to death. Zhu Gengsheng had also committed the crime of violating the same regulations and should be sentenced to life imprisonment. However, considering his ignorance, the court decided to apply Article 14, Article 44, Item 1, Article 77, and Article 80, Item 2 of the same regulations, reducing the sentence by half and sentencing him to eight years of imprisonment. The case was submitted to the Nanchang Camp for review and approval. Chiang Kai-shek approved the case and ordered that the two criminals, Feng and Zhu, be returned to the county government of this county for execution. Yesterday (15th) morning at 9:00 a.m., County Magistrate Yan presided over the case and ordered Feng A'ren to be brought to the court to confirm his identity. He was then tied up and taken to the South School Field for execution by firing squad.

Changzhou 96

Drug Dealers

Yang Chuan'er and Zhao Shijun Executed

Yang Chuan'er, a major seller of drug pills, previously operated a Yunshi thread shop in Hualong Lane. The Public Security Bureau sent police to search his home. Yang himself heard the news and escaped, leaving only his accomplice, who was immediately sent to the court for trial. Subsequently, the court and the Public Security Bureau immediately issued a warrant for Yang Chuan'er's arrest. To avoid the authorities' attention and to evade punishment, his family falsely reported his death to the county court. In August of this year, the Public Security Bureau, based on information from the Huzhou branch, arrested Zhao Shijun, a seller of drug pills. During the preliminary hearing, Zhao confessed that all the drug pills were purchased from Yang Chuan'er at No. 3 Xichengjiaobu. Director Xu Baoguang of the bureau immediately sent officers to take Zhao Shijun to the address for investigation and arrest. As a result, Yang Chuan'er and the drug-making equipment were seized and brought to the bureau for interrogation. Yang confessed without hesitation and said that there was human evidence and that he was awaiting execution. Both Zhao and Yang were handed over to the county, and then to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for trial. After the trial, it was confirmed that they were guilty, and they were returned to the original county for imprisonment. On the 24th, the county government received an order from the Provincial Garrison Headquarters, relayed by the Nanchang Camp, approving the death sentence. That afternoon, police were dispatched to extract Yang and Zhao from prison, verify their identities, and take them to the Xiwudun execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Older Brother Kicks Younger Brother to Death 97

Outside the West Gate, on the street of Pengbu, west of the second section, next to the river in front of the Jiusi Fire Station, there were several fishing boats moored. The boat owners were two brothers, the older brother named Wang Quansheng (50 years old) and the younger brother named Wang Quanbao (46 years old). Each had a wife, children, and an elderly mother, Ding (70+ years old), all living on the boats. Early the day before yesterday, the brothers and their wives each took their catch of fish and shrimp to sell near the Tianhou Palace market on the Dashi Bridge. Because the two brothers fought over customers, they started fighting. Wang Quansheng kicked Wang Quanbao in the lower abdomen, causing him to fall and get injured. Wang Quansheng was brought to the 9th Precinct of the Public Security Bureau and was fined 5 yuan. Wang Quanbao was ordered to return for treatment. After Quanbao returned to the boat, he was in severe abdominal pain and went to the Xiongbei Hospital for treatment. Surgeons such as Chen Fu and others were consulted, but to no avail. Yesterday morning, he died. Quansheng, seeing that he had caused the disaster, immediately fled. The 4th Precinct of the Public Security Bureau learned of the incident and immediately sent police to investigate. Since the perpetrator was on the run, the police took the deceased's mother, Ding, and wife, Fang, to the station for questioning. The 27th Tuzheng Chen Zizhao of the area reported the incident to the local branch court. An inspector was dispatched to examine the body and confirmed that he had died from injuries sustained before death. The inspector ordered the family of the deceased to collect the body and await the arrest of the perpetrator.

Nantong 98

Nantong and Rugao Fishermen Defend Themselves Against Bandits

In the coastal areas of Nantong and Rugao, sea bandits are rampant. The two counties have organized a maritime patrol to suppress them. On one hand, fishermen are defending themselves. The Nantong District Security Commander has formulated measures: (1) Ship Registration: All coastal vessels, regardless of whether they are warships or fishing boats, must be registered by the coastal district chiefs of Nantong and Rugao counties, and numbered certificates will be issued. (2) Baojia System: Each boat will have a captain, and every ten boats will elect a jiazhang to handle local autonomy and self-defense matters. Each county's jiazhang will elect one deputy baozhang, who may set up a baozhang office on land. (Rest omitted).

Rugao 99

Fierce Battle between Soldiers and Bandits in Juegang

On the morning of the 14th of this month, near Dongguan Doutingzi in Juegang District, Rugao, twelve warships suddenly encountered eight bandit ships moored in the sand in the sea. A fierce battle ensued. After six hours, the official soldiers seized seven bandit ships and destroyed one, killing more than 100 bandits. The fishermen were pleased. On the 10th, more than ten bandits in plain clothes suddenly arrived at the house of Wu Qianmao, a villager in the 8th Township of Juegang, hiding firearms in sacks. The head of the township and the director of the sentry station, Wang, received the news and immediately dispatched more than 20 people from the 8th and 10th sentry stations to arrest them. The bandits fled upon hearing the news. After chasing them for more than a mile to the south, four people, Shi Lixue, Zhang Changli, Yao He, and Liu Zhu, were arrested and sent to the county for strict investigation.

Refugees Rob Wealthy Household 100

Chen Tinggan, a villager in Tongren Township, 4th District, makes a living by farming and owns hundreds of acres of land, making him the wealthiest man in the township. The day before yesterday afternoon, more than 100 refugees from Hunan passed by his house and demanded rice. When Chen refused, they shouted and rushed into the house, overturning boxes and cabinets and searching at will. When the villagers learned of this, they beat gongs and gathered the crowd to confront the refugees. Seeing that the situation was unfavorable, the refugees left in formation. After checking, it was found that more than 1,000 yuan in cash, clothes, ornaments, etc. were lost. The incident has been reported to the county government for investigation.

Ningbo 101

Robbery at Xizhu Nunnery in Hongtang

Li Maozhang from Cixi was feigning to fast and worship Buddha at Xizhu Nunnery in Hongtang the day before yesterday. Yesterday (23rd) at 1:00 AM, suddenly six or seven bandits broke in and stole ninety ten-yuan notes, more than twenty five-yuan notes, more than forty one-yuan notes from the Industry Bank, a gold watch, and a gold chain that Li was carrying. The incident was reported to the nearby Public Security Bureau for investigation. It is unknown if the bandits will be caught.

Wuhu 102

Huge Amount of Smuggled Opium Discovered on EWO Steamer in Wuhu

The British-owned EWO steamer, Jih Wo, which operates on the Yangtze River, sailed from Hankou a few days ago. Someone secretly transported a large amount of smuggled opium onto the ship and hid it in the hold, intending to unload it at a certain port downstream. However, the plan was discovered. Three people abandoned the ship and came to Wuhu the day before. Li Xiping, the Wuhu Special Commissioner of the Northern Jiangsu Inspectorate, was tipped off and signed a guarantee that if the information was false, he would offer one person to be punished with death. Li specially dispatched a commissioner to investigate, because the amount of smuggled opium was too large. In addition to asking the Wuhu Special Tax Office to send police to assist, he also went to the Customs and discussed with Customs Commissioner Lauton. When the ship arrived in Wuhu, Li, accompanied by the new Customs River Patrol Director Locke, led customs officers and police to board the ship. Guided by informants, they searched the ship and discovered a large iron plate in the bottom of the coal bunker, behind which there was another door. There were many footprints, and based on the coal loading situation, there should not be many people other than the stoker coming and going to this place. Judging the size of the footprints, it was decided to open the door to investigate. As soon as the door was opened, stacks of sacks were displayed before their eyes. At that moment, a stoker took the opportunity to throw a cloth bag wrapped in oilcloth into the river and fled. Therefore, the River Patrol Director and Commissioner Li ordered the police officers to check the contents of the sacks and confirmed that they were the reported unstamped smuggled opium, a total of forty-seven pieces, with more than seven additional pieces, each weighing about ninety pounds, totaling more than forty stones. At the current opium price, it is worth as much as 120,000 yuan. In addition to sending personnel to monitor the unloading, the shipowner was contacted and asked to hand over the smugglers and suspicious stokers for thorough investigation. Subsequently, the stoker was handed over, and the ship was allowed to sail. The captured smuggled opium and suspects have been taken to the office of the Li Special Commissioner for investigation. (24th)

Page 9

Local News: H.H. Kung Discusses National Unity

Wang Chonghui Conveys Opinions, Misunderstandings Cleared; H.H. Kung to Inspect the North As Soon As Government Affairs Permit 103

Central News Agency reports: H.H. Kung, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, left Nanjing by night train at 11:00 p.m. on the 24th and arrived at Zhenru at 7:15 a.m. on the 25th. He got off the train and went straight to his private residence on Rue de l'Amiral Bayle to rest. At 10:30 a.m., he met with newspaper reporters at his residence. At 11:00 a.m., he went to offer condolences at the funeral of Madam Wang Boqun. At noon, he went to the Central Bank to handle important official business. H.H. Kung's remarks are recorded as follows:

Will Go North When Time Permits 104

According to H.H. Kung, he will go to the north as soon as government affairs permit, to inspect the Yellow River water conservancy project, the financial situation in North China, handle Mingxian school affairs, and take care of personal matters. As for the date of departure, it has not yet been decided. What I can tell you is that as soon as I have time, I will set off.

National Spiritual Unity 105

Mr. Wang Chonghui felt deeply after returning from overseas that there is no way to save the country without national spiritual unity. Mr. Wang is a world-renowned scholar, a former responsible official in the government, and a veteran comrade in the Kuomintang. Therefore, he visited comrades from all sides to exchange opinions in order to seek national unity. In the past, comrades in and out of the government often had misunderstandings due to estrangement and blamed each other. Since Mr. Wang conveyed the opinions of all parties to each other, misunderstandings can be cleared up. As for whether Mr. Wang will go south again, I have not heard of it.

Silver Tax Increase Issue 106

There have been many rumors since the silver tax increase, saying that the government is implementing centralized cash collection, inflating currency, reducing the fineness of silver coins, and implementing the gold standard. Minister Kung denied this, saying that the implementation of the silver tax increase was originally to prevent the large-scale outflow of silver. The intention is very clear. Therefore, in addition to the prescribed tax rate, a balancing tax is added, which increases or decreases with the price at any time, so that merchants have no profit to be made. Rumors such as currency inflation and reducing the fineness of silver coins are all speculations from the outside world. Paper money in various countries is all issued by the government, and silver is all collected in the treasury. Therefore, it is possible to reduce the fineness of the standard currency and inflate the currency with a single order. Silver coins in our country circulate in the market, and in fact, they cannot be collected from the people and then changed to reduce the silver content. Moreover, the silver content of issued silver coins is stipulated by law, so how can it be changed casually?

Jiangsu Provincial Public Bonds Pledged for Loans Agreed Upon

Various Banks Organize Committee, Zhao Dihua to Come to Shanghai to Sign 107

Central News Agency reports: The Jiangsu Province's 23rd Year Water Conservancy Construction Public Bonds' pledge to various banks in Shanghai has been largely agreed upon after two visits by Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Department. The amount of loans to be recognized by each bank has also been negotiated by Xu Baoying, General Manager of Jiangsu Bank. Director Zhao has set a date to come to Shanghai again to formally sign the contract. The details of the pledge amount are recorded below:

Loan Amount 108

The total amount of the Jiangsu Province's 23rd Year Water Conservancy Construction Public Bonds is 20 million yuan. After being approved by the Executive Yuan, Director Zhao Dihua of the Finance Department came to Shanghai to negotiate with the banking community for a pledge because of the urgent need for funds. It was agreed that in addition to fully recovering the 2 million yuan worth of bonds issued by the province in previous years, a face value of 12.5 million yuan would be pledged to various banks at a 60% discount, totaling 7.5 million yuan. At the same time, as a result of Director Zhao's negotiations with Central Bank President H.H. Kung, the Central Bank is also willing to pledge 1 million yuan at half price for 500,000 yuan. The remaining 4.5 million yuan will be raised by Jiangsu Province by soliciting 2 million yuan from local gentry and merchants, and 2.5 million yuan will be allocated for river engineering construction and will be issued or pledged by the River Engineering Bureau itself.

To Sign Contract 109

After Director Zhao reached an agreement with various banks on the total amount of the pledge, he first returned to Zhen. Xu Baoying, General Manager of Jiangsu Bank, represented the province in Shanghai to negotiate the amount of recognition with various banks. The provincial government also sent personnel to various inland banks in Suzhou and Jiading to negotiate separately. Although each bank has not fully recognized the amount, it has been largely agreed upon. Director Zhao will come to Shanghai within a few days to sign the contract. However, it has not been decided whether each bank will sign a joint or separate contract. The interest rate is set at 8%, and the term is undecided.

Organizing Committee 110

After this loan is completed, the banks will form a syndicate, with the Bank of China as the representative, in order to facilitate negotiations. A committee will also be organized, with the participating banks and the Jiangsu Provincial authorities participating. However, the candidates for the committee have not yet been decided. It is also heard that the bond certificates for the public bonds have been priced at Commercial Press and Chung Hwa Book Company.

Ministry of Finance Suppresses Foreign Exchange Settlement, Central Bank Ordered to Comply

Exiled Overseas Chinese from Japan Send Representatives to Petition in Nanjing Yesterday 123

The Eleventh Group Will Arrive in Shanghai Today

Our overseas Chinese in Japan have been repeatedly expelled. After returning to Shanghai, due to the difficulty of making a living, they have petitioned various party and government agencies for relief, and appealed to various schools. Yesterday, the overseas Chinese in Shanghai specially sent the tenth group of returning representatives, led by Wang Yanqian, to Nanjing to petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the National Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. Their goals are: (1) to provide immediate relief to maintain their livelihoods; (2) to negotiate with the Japanese government to return confiscated property; (3) to establish the Overseas Chinese Village ahead of schedule so that the overseas Chinese can have a place to live. They will return to Shanghai after receiving approval. As for the eleventh group of overseas Chinese, their Japanese ship, Rokko Maru, is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 2:00 PM today.

Relief Association Asks Ministry of Finance to Approve Draft of Disaster Relief Preparation Regulations 125

The Shanghai Drought Relief Association for Various Provinces, due to the severe drought in various provinces, telegraphed Minister Kong yesterday, requesting that the regulations on the Management Committee for Disaster Relief Reserve Funds and other implementing regulations be quickly reviewed and promulgated. The original text is as follows: "To Minister Kong of the Nanjing Ministry of Finance: The drought in various provinces this year is extremely severe, and relief is urgently needed. We, while we still have a breath, cannot delay relief. Therefore, we have organized a Drought Relief Association for various provinces to do our best to alleviate the disaster. We also hope that you, as the appointed president, will bring happiness to the victims. We have long been aware that floods and droughts are common, and disaster relief is always difficult. Preparation is essential. At this time of national difficulty, whenever a disaster occurs, both the government and society are concerned. Even with every effort, the results are still limited. The victims cannot wait for relief, and will inevitably resort to fleeing. The cash from the countryside is flowing into the cities, and the concentration in the cities is flowing overseas. Production is failing, and income is exceeding expenditures. Furthermore, unrest is increasing, and taxes are increasing daily. The economy of the countryside is collapsing, and the foundation of society is gradually shaking. As the saying goes, 'If the people are not sufficient, how can the ruler be sufficient?' Looking ahead, our worries are endless. We have found that the Central Relief Committee previously presented to the National Government the Disaster Relief Reserve System, which is used in Japan and the United States, to formulate the Disaster Relief Reserve Fund Law, stipulating that the central government should set aside one percent of its total expenditure annually, and the provinces two percent, as a disaster relief reserve fund, to be used exclusively for disaster relief and prevention, included in the budget, and not to be diverted. The Legislative Yuan formulated the Disaster Relief Reserve Fund Law on October 28 of the 19th year, so that the country's ability to provide disaster relief can be strengthened in peacetime, and the losses from disasters in various places will be restored in a short time. We hope that the implementation will be accelerated. We have heard that the regulations on the Management Committee and the implementing regulations were drafted by the Relief Committee of the Ministry of Interior after the promulgation of the law, and sent to the Ministry for detailed review, but have not yet been implemented. We deeply appreciate your compassion and concern, and believe that you will pay special attention to detailed planning. We sincerely request that you approve the draft regulations as soon as possible, and request implementation, and order all provinces to organize in accordance with the law. This would be like removing firewood and bending chimneys, allowing the government to make great plans for the years to come, and allowing us to avoid future failures. As the saying goes, 'When benevolent people are in power, there will be no starving people in the country.' We look forward to your favorable response. Xu Shiying, Wang Zhengting, Wang..., Wu Tiecheng, Chu Fucheng, Wen Lanting, Zhang Yin, Du..., Wang Xiaofan, and others kowtow together."

Severe Disaster Situation in Wuwei County, Anhui 129

The Shanghai Branch of the World Red Swastika Society released information about the disaster situation in Wuwei County, Anhui, stating that the disaster and the suffering of the people are unprecedented. Since the collapse of the river embankment in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the flood has caused disasters, and livestock and fields have been almost completely submerged. The morale of the people has not yet recovered, and the situation is dire. Unexpectedly, after the flood, there was a poor harvest, followed by drought. This year, in the summer, the drought devastated the crops, and the streams and ponds were dry. All cotton, sesame, beans, sweet potatoes, and other crops have no harvest to speak of, and even the areas for drinking water are dry. The dry farmland covers more than 229,400 mu, and the dry small embankments and high slopes cover more than 142,500 mu. The total affected farmland is more than 371,300 mu, and the affected population is more than 200,000. They are starving and waiting to be fed. It is unbearable to hear that some are too hungry to go out, some fathers abandon their sons and husbands abandon their wives, and some sell their children to survive. There are even those who die of starvation along the way. It is unbearable to see. We hope that kind people and philanthropists will show compassion and provide relief funds and food to the disaster area, so that the dying people can be rescued and be grateful.

Public Works Department Collects Land Tax 135

No Shortfall in Collections This Year

According to the report on tax revenue published by the Public Works Department this Friday, the total land tax collected up to the end of September was 4,671,638.46 yuan for the first nine months of this year. Compared with last year, a total of 5,793,357.51 yuan was collected up to the end of September last year. The difference between the two numbers seems to be significant. The reason is that after the revaluation of land prices last year, in order to take care of taxpayers, they were allowed to pay 80% of the increased amount in the second half of the year, but it had to be paid before the end of September to be valid. Therefore, more than 3 million yuan was collected in September alone last year. This year, only more than 190,000 yuan was collected in September. At the end of September last year, the outstanding amount was only 112,000 yuan. At the end of September this year, the outstanding amount was still 2,341,000 yuan.

Two Telegraph Bureaus Announce Cancellation of Unregistered Simplified Character Telegrams 137

Effective from the First of Next Month

The International Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau hereby notify all sectors regarding telegraph registration: According to the order of the Ministry of Communications, the trial delivery method stipulated in Article 19 of the Telegraph Registration Regulations should be cancelled from October 1. All incoming telegrams that use a single simplified character as the name and address of the recipient without being registered in accordance with the regulations should be handled as undeliverable telegrams. Therefore, from November 1 of this year, all unregistered telegrams will be invalid and will no longer be delivered. If you have not yet registered or your registration has expired and you have not continued to register in accordance with the regulations, please go to the United Telegraph Registration Office at 70 Fuzhou Road in this city, or the receiving and dispatching offices of the International Radio Station, and the receiving and dispatching offices of the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific submarine cables to register in accordance with the regulations. Please do not make a mistake.

French Concession Promulgates Regulations for the Management of Public Passenger Vehicles 139

The Shanghai French Municipal Council, in accordance with Article 13 of its organizational charter, promulgated the Regulations for the Management of Public Passenger Vehicles by the Shanghai French Municipal Council, published by the French Consul General in Shanghai, which contains 19 lengthy articles. Violators of these regulations shall be subject to a fine of between one and five hundred yuan by the competent court. The Chief of the Police of the Municipal Council may detain or revoke the driver's license of a driver who violates the regulations, neglects his duties, or causes an accident. In the event of a serious crime, the Bureau shall have the right to withhold or revoke the license and file a complaint against the licensee or driver.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Issues Order: Cooperatives Must Be Organized in Accordance with the Law 140

Illegal Cooperatives Will Be Strictly Banned

Establishment Permitted Only When Strictly Following the Cooperative Law

The establishment of cooperatives was originally intended to benefit the public, achieve mutual assistance, and jointly seek the interests of the members. However, recently, a few unscrupulous people have used the name of cooperatives to operate like ordinary stores. In order to rectify the situation, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs previously issued an order urging all cooperatives to register. Over time, more than fifty or sixty have registered. However, in fact, the number is definitely more than this. The registration period has now expired. Those with pure purposes and legal organizations will be approved and guided by the Bureau of Social Affairs. Others who use the name of cooperatives for private gain will be strictly banned to avoid abuses. The Bureau also stipulates that the Cooperative Law has nine chapters, including general rules for establishment, members' shares and surpluses, directors, supervisors and staff, meetings, dissolution and liquidation, cooperative unions, penalties, and supplementary rules. In order to facilitate agriculture, industry, finance, and mutual assistance among members, it is possible to establish production, consumption, and disease, disaster, life and death insurance cooperatives. The responsibilities are divided into three types: limited, unlimited, and guaranteed. There must be a minimum of seven people, and there must be no corrupt behavior. The Bureau of Social Affairs now also issues a notice that all organizations wishing to establish cooperatives must strictly comply with the regulations before they are allowed to be established.

Woman Journalist and Sociologist Miss Wang Xiaomeng to Return Home 144

Miss Wang Xiaomeng, of Hangzhou County, graduated from Shanghai University in the twentieth year of the Republic (1931). Last summer, she went to the United States and studied at the University of Southern California. This summer, she obtained a Master's degree in Journalism. The university's granting of a Master's degree in Journalism began with Miss Wang, making her the only student at the university since its founding to receive this honorary degree. Her graduation thesis is titled "A Comparison of the History of Journalism in China and the United States." The thesis is now listed in the university's new medical collection.

Miss Wang also excels in sociology and has studied with the famous American sociologist Mr. Bogardus, conducting investigations into the life and status of overseas Chinese in the Green Core region of the Rocky Mountains in the United States. Furthermore, she frequently publishes papers in American sociological journals.

Wang Xiaomeng

While Miss Wang was in the United States, the Los Angeles Daily News also frequently published her translated works. Miss Wang always aimed to promote national friendship and raise the status of Chinese women. Because many foreigners were ignorant of Chinese culture and history, often regarding China as an ancient country lacking brilliance and isolated from the new era, Miss Wang did her best to promote China through this newspaper. At the same time, she also gave speeches at various women's groups and literary societies, always receiving great acclaim. Therefore, the Green Core Daily News once wrote, "Miss Wang Xiaomeng is the new China."

Miss Wang also enjoyed socializing with people from all walks of life and was friendly with several famous American movie stars and directors. Hollywood often saw her presence throughout the year. In addition, Miss Wang frequently visited both journalism and academic circles. After leaving the United States, Miss Wang went to Europe to study the European newspaper industry and customs. She visited Italy, France, England, Germany, Belgium, and Switzerland. While in Italy, Miss Wang also studied Fascism and published an article in an English newspaper in Shanghai about the shortcomings and applications of this ideology. She also studied Italian. It is now heard that Miss Wang has boarded an Italian liner to return home and is expected to arrive in Shanghai in early November.

Miss Wang's return to China will not only bring honor to China's women's circles but will also contribute to China's newspaper industry.

Chen Sixuan's Paintings Exhibited Yesterday, Marking a Pioneering Event for Women's Solo Exhibitions in China 145

Miss Chen Sixuan of Min County is skilled in painting and calligraphy, with a reputation that extends both at home and abroad. Her works have been featured at the Chicago Exposition and the Sino-German painting exhibition in previous years. Recently, at the invitation of famous figures in Shanghai, she is exhibiting her masterpieces created over the years on the third floor of the Continental Emporium on Nanjing Road. The display is dazzling and breathtaking. Among them are pieces like "A Red Tree and Green Mountains, Good for Launching a Boat," "Mountain Rain is Coming, Wind Fills the Tower," "Reading the Book of Changes by the Autumn Window," and "A Group of Immortals Offer Tribute," each of which is nearly indistinguishable from the works of Wang Yuanqi and Yun Shouping. Yesterday, people from all walks of life visited in an endless stream. A solo exhibition of paintings by a woman is still a pioneering event in China.

China Library Encyclopedia Editorial Office to Organize an Exhibition of Manuscript Materials 146

The China Library Encyclopedia Editorial Office was established in February of the twentieth year of the Republic (1931) with three objectives: First, to establish a purely academic enterprise of collation and criticism, to take stock of Chinese culture and scholarship, to understand the richness of past achievements, to critique the merits of current trends, and to determine the direction of future efforts. Second, to introduce all books and scholars, ancient and modern, to the reading public, and to collect, collate, and verify criticisms and records of books and authors to provide convenience to the academic community. Third, to compile a Chinese encyclopedia and other academic reference books to facilitate knowledge acquisition and foster a love of reading. Since its establishment, the founder, Mr. Yang Jialuo, has donated funds totaling 20,700 yuan. The books compiled and printed include Yang's own "Dictionary of the Four Libraries," "Book Yearbook," "Supplement to the Book Yearbook," "Bibliography," "Dictionary of Books," "Portraits of Famous Figures of the Republic," "Dictionary of Qing Dynasty Figures," "Dictionary of Chinese Literature," "Dictionary of the Confucian Classics," "Simplified Anthology of Early Tang Poetry," and "Records of Ink Sea Classics," "Eulogy to Mr. Gao Qifeng," "Paintings of Miss Zhang Kunyi," etc. Each of Yang's ten books contains between two and three million words, truly a monumental work of the Chinese academic community. The total number of words is over twenty million, equivalent to the weight of the twenty-four histories which contained over three thousand and two hundred volumes. The Chairman of the National Government and the heads of various ministries, provincial governors, and directors of education have all presented inscriptions. The education departments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Shandong, Hebei, Henan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Guangdong, Guangxi, Fujian, Yunnan, Chahar, and Suiyuan provinces, as well as the municipal education bureaus of Nanjing, Beiping, and other cities, have ordered that these books be provided for reference. There have been over forty such orders. Professor Zhang Liangsi of England, Professor Asher Joel of the United States, Professor Alick of Russia, and Professor Jitsui Keishu of Japan, all renowned scholars in the world, have written lengthy criticisms published in magazines. The books compiled by the Editorial Office have been successively published and have already attracted serious attention from academic circles both at home and abroad. Therefore, it has been decided to publicly exhibit the manuscripts and materials accumulated over the years to seek criticism from the public. The preparations for this exhibition are now underway, and it is scheduled to open in December. Among the exhibits, the following are said to be the most noteworthy: First, the manuscripts of the published "Dictionary of the Four Libraries," "Book Yearbook," "Dictionary of Qing Dynasty Figures," "Dictionary of Chinese Literature," and "Dictionary of Confucian Classics," totaling over seven hundred volumes. Second, over two hundred thousand cards containing the index cards and bottom cards for the published "Bibliography" and "Dictionary of Books," divided into thirty cases. Third, over seventy volumes of manuscripts of the published "Portraits of Famous Figures of the Republic" and over two thousand photographs of the autographs of over two thousand famous figures from across the country, as well as over one hundred and fifty thousand index cards of newspapers from various regions since the founding of the Republic and over two thousand collected materials, all of which are extremely valuable materials for the modern history of our country. Fourth, over one hundred volumes of drafts and over one hundred volumes of manuscripts of the "Early Anthology of Tang Poetry," a portion of which has been selected and printed. Fifth, the posthumous works and photographs of Mr. Gao Qifeng, revered by Chairman Lin as the Holy Sage, and the paintings of his daughter, Miss Zhang Kunyi. Sixth, over seven hundred criticisms from home and abroad of Yang's ten books, as well as thirty volumes of Yang's records of reading and compiling the "Complete Library of the Four Treasuries" of over thirty-six thousand volumes over the past ten years and of visiting over twenty thousand books in over a dozen provinces. An exhibition of manuscripts and materials is still a pioneering event in our country, and these manuscripts and materials are of great significance to our country's academic and modern history. It is believed that the exhibition will have a tremendous impact on the future of our country's academia.

After the bankruptcy of the China Industrial Bank, the manager, Bao Yuan, absconded with funds in advance. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui summoned the private plaintiffs, Qian Zunmin, and ordered the defendant Lu Xihou, who was in custody, to be brought to court, after announcing this proposition, the private prosecution of Qian and others was immediately dismissed by the court, and they were ordered to report the facts of the defendant's embezzlement and fraud to the patrol room and await public prosecution, which has been recorded in this newspaper. It is now learned that the measures announced by the First Special Court apply to general creditors who wish to file private prosecutions after the bank's bankruptcy. If the private prosecution case was filed before the bank's bankruptcy, it will still be tried separately and will not be included in the public prosecution case. Therefore, the private prosecution dismissed by Judge Liu the day before yesterday afternoon was only Qian Zunmin's case against Lu Xihou. The Ministry of Communications believes that foreign vessel inspection is of great importance to China's maritime rights. Increase in Population in the French Concession

An Increase of 1,657 People Compared to Last Year, with White Russians, Americans, and French Being the Most Numerous Among Foreigners 153

According to a recent population survey by the French Public Works Bureau, the total population of the French Concession is 498,193, of which 18,899 are of foreign nationality and 479,294 are of Chinese nationality. The total population has increased by 1,657 people compared to last year, of which foreigners have increased by 1,118 people and Chinese have increased by 1,657 people. As for foreign nationalities: (1) White Russian 8,260 people, British 2,630 people, American 1,792 people, French 1,430 people, Hungarian 980 people, German 725 people, Portuguese 412 people, Japanese 280 people, Polish 261 people, Danish 194 people, in addition, Argentinian, Belgian, Chilean, Cuban, Egyptian, Bulgarian, Finnish, Indian, Greek, Norwegian, Swiss, Yugoslavian, Czechoslovakian, Persian, Swedish, Romanian, Hungarian, Spanish, and Irish nationals are all in the minority. As for the increase in population, the most numerous foreign nationality is White Russian, an increase of 1,017 people compared to last year, followed by French, German, British, Italian, and other nationals. There has been a significant decrease in the number of Americans and Japanese residing in the French Concession. Furthermore, on average, there is a fifteen-year-old child in every seven Chinese families living in the French Concession.

Her statement roughly states that the plaintiff is a weak, unsophisticated country girl who, despite being over twenty years old, is still unmarried. Later, she discovered that the defendant's wife was still alive and that he was violent and often beat her. On August 23 of this year, the plaintiff's mother took her back home. For self-preservation, she has no choice but to terminate the relationship. However, the defendant's fraudulent actions have caused her to lose her reputation and integrity. Like a withered flower and fallen leaf, who will pity her? Facing a bleak future, life is extremely difficult. She requests living expenses of three thousand yuan. The plaintiff holds assets of three hundred and eighty-nine yuan, etc. The defendant, Zhu Jiaxiang, hired lawyer Pan Zhensheng to file a defense, roughly stating that the defendant is approaching middle age and, for the sake of continuing his lineage, agreed on November 13, 1933, to take the plaintiff as a concubine. He sent her two hundred yuan in gifts, a gold bracelet, two gold rings, and a pair of gold bangles. The original date for her to enter his household was December 26. Later, a Jin Zhuolun appeared and objected, claiming that taking a concubine was too cheap and that an additional six hundred yuan was required. The defendant had no choice but to send the full amount. Unexpectedly, after only a little over half a year, the plaintiff was taken away by her mother, requesting fulfillment of the agreement. He refutes the plaintiff's lawsuit and requests a judgment ordering them to live together, etc. The case was heard yesterday by Judge Xu. The plaintiff testified about the previous events. The defendant did not appear; only lawyer Pan represented him in court. After the defense was presented, the judge ordered an adjournment for further hearing.

Still smiling, they entered the court and stood in their positions as plaintiff and defendant. At the same time, relatives and friends of both parties, as well as lawyers and court staff, also attended the hearing, making the courtroom very crowded. The judge first asked the plaintiff, Cai Xiaobai, about the object of the lawsuit. Cai answered that it was based on Articles 1052, Section 3, 4, and 6 of the Civil Code, requesting a divorce decree and stating various reasons for not being able to live together. She claimed that Wu Julij indeed committed the sixteen points of abuse against elders, attempted murder, and tampering with case files listed in the complaint, and locking her in a room to prevent her from appearing in court, etc. The judge then questioned the defendant, Wu Julij, based on this. According to his statement, he is twenty-six years old, from Changzhou, and his relationship with the plaintiff, Cai Xiaobai, was entirely based on love. However, his personality is irritable, and he admits to knowing this, but marital disputes are very common matters. However, out of consideration for her reputation, he dared not hit her. She now wants a divorce, and he cannot agree. Moreover, last night she was still with him at the Dayi Apartment. He said her considerations were all incorrect. After the judge reviewed the statements, he ordered the closing arguments to begin, which were then concluded. The verdict is scheduled to be announced on the afternoon of the 30th. The plaintiff remained smiling as she left the courtroom, accompanied by her relatives and friends.

From beginning to end, there was no mention of anyone related to Liang Chengyu. Moreover, when the perpetrators of the kidnapping of Chen Shifan, Wu Shenxian, etc., were identified in court, they all claimed not to know Liang Chengyu. This is the only conclusive evidence for Liang's appeal and should lead to a declaration of the appellant Liang Chengyu's innocence. (2) Regarding the original trial's use of Li Liansheng's testimony as the basis for the judgment, the testimony of Li Liansheng was entirely false and inconsistent throughout. This further proves Liang's innocence. In the original trial, evidence favorable to the defendant was not adopted, and the original judgment was based on legally unfounded testimony, suggesting bias and a factual error. It is requested that the original judgment be overturned according to law and a new judgment be issued, declaring the appellant Liang Chengyu innocent, etc. The Second Branch of the High Court has concluded its hearing. Yesterday afternoon, Presiding Judge Yu Hua, along with Judges Zhao and Zhou, appeared in court to announce the judgment. The main text stated that the part of the original judgment concerning the conviction and sentence is overturned, and Liang Chengyu is innocent.
